After Fu Zuoyi Goes to Dengkou, Peaceful Atmosphere Intensifies 2

Sun Dianying Plans to Go to Taiyuan and Reside Temporarily

Please Do Not Have Ma Hongkui Pursue

He [Yingqin] Calls Generals to Discuss Military Affairs

No Attacks During Negotiations

(Beiping) He Yingqin Invited Senior Generals in Beiping, including Wan Fulin, Shang Zhen, Xu Yongchang, Pang Bingxun, etc., to a meeting at Jurentang at 10 a.m. on the 2nd to discuss the aftermath of Sun's troops. Decisions depended on the results of Sun and Fu's trip. If satisfactory, the three items explained in the telegrams of the three commissioners Pang, Hu, and Ji could be handled. If Sun still refuses to leave the military and makes further demands, a joint encirclement and suppression by a large army will be implemented immediately. During the peaceful negotiation period of the Sun incident, the Northwest authorities will only encircle and not attack. Therefore, there are no fierce battles at the front. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) According to a certain source, Sun's army did once occupy Ningyuan, but due to the joint counterattack of the Four Mas, they withdrew again. Now, Sun has decided to reside in Taiyuan, and his troops will be stationed, reorganized, and reduced in size along the borders of Gansu, Ningxia, and Suiyuan, as determined by Pang and others. He has requested Ma Hongkui not to send troops to pursue, and telegraphed Ma, stating that there was a misunderstanding and that he has decided to reside temporarily in Taiyuan, asking that room be left for future meetings and ordering that no troops be sent in pursuit, etc. Ma has telegraphed this intention, and it is expected that after Fu Zhankui and others arrive at the front, the peaceful resolution plan can be materialized. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Fu Zuoyi, accompanied by Fu Zhankui, Men Bingyue, and senior staff officers of the military commission, Zhang Xuanze and Wang Zhongquan, arrived in Suiyuan on the 1st. On the 2nd, they telegraphed Beiping, reporting that Li Ming had already gone to Baotou to take a car prepared by the provincial government to Dengkou to negotiate the aftermath of Sun's troops. Fu, Zhang, and Wang will change trains at 2 p.m. on the 2nd to Baotou and then Dengkou to meet Sun. Men will remain in Suiyuan temporarily to handle all military liaison tasks. Fu will go to the front in three or four days to supervise military affairs. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) A certain member of the military commission said that Fu Zhankui went to Suiyuan with handwritten letters from He, Pang, Hu, and Ji, which mainly stated that Fu would go to discuss everything in person and verbally convey their sincere advice, believing that at this time of national crisis, he should consider the overall situation, prioritize the country, pull back from the brink, and not be despised by the people of the country. The outcome of Fu's trip is difficult to predict, but it is generally believed that Sun personally may not have great difficulties. Whether his subordinates will obey is uncertain and cannot be immediately judged. There is no full assurance. If Sun is determined to leave the military, Fu will also accompany him to Taiyuan. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) He Yingqin received a telegram from Fu Zuoyi today, reporting that Zhao Chengzhou's cavalry troops had opened up to Baotou and were advancing towards Linhe. After receiving the telegram here, he ordered Fu to command the various units to continue westward. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Ma Hongkui telegraphed Beiping, reporting that the various units of Sun's army had repeatedly failed in their attacks and no longer had the ability to counterattack. Sun had indeed gone to the front to supervise the troops a few days ago, but due to the unfavorable war situation, he has returned to the rear to reorganize the remnants. The war situation in Ningxia and Pingluo has not changed significantly. In addition, a certain officer of Sun's army talked to Beiping, saying that Yu Shiming's cavalry had largely bypassed Ningxia and advanced south, with the vanguard reaching Zhongwei. Two brigades of Sun's infantry are currently stationed in Ningsuo. Ningxia is defended by Ma Lin leading a division. Most of Sun's rear is concentrated west of Dengkou, which is defended by Sun's Peng Zhenguo's troops. (2nd Special Telegram)

Ma Yinchu's Opinion on the Silver Agreement 3

Advocates Not Approving It

(Nanjing) Ma Yinchu's opinion and thoughts on the Silver Agreement are over 3,000 words long. The conclusion is that it is best not to approve the Silver Agreement. Moreover, the United States itself has not fulfilled the agreement, buying 10 million ounces per month for ten consecutive months, totaling 100 million ounces, which has destroyed the balance of supply and demand. How can China be forced to comply? This is the first point. Previously, when the price of US gold was high, the value of its gold coins was also reduced, about 60% of the previous value. Previously, one ounce of pure gold could be exchanged for 23 US dollars, but now it is 35 US dollars, and there are even advocates for 40 US dollars. Then its fineness is already below 800/1000 in the standard currency. How can China be forced not to reduce the fineness of its gold coins to below 800/1000? This is the second point. If the agreement is to be approved, free conditional conditions should be added. The proposed clause is as follows: "If the price of silver rises sharply and has an adverse impact on China's finance and industry, the Chinese government, out of necessity to protect industry and reform the currency system, shall be free to take appropriate actions." On the one hand, please jointly study with national industrial and commercial leaders and economic experts, such as Gu Jigao, Sun Zeng, Liu Dajun, Liu Zhendong, Huang Yuanyi, and Bai Aide. All six of them need to be consulted. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Silver Agreement was not submitted for discussion at the Legislative Yuan's general meeting on the 2nd and is still under review by the Economic, Finance, and Foreign Affairs committees. According to a certain committee member, the case was sent to the Legislative Yuan on the morning of the 1st, and a joint meeting was held by the three committees in the afternoon to review it. President Wang also sent a member to the meeting to report. At that time, some members believed that the case was of great importance and could not be completed in a hasty review, and they advocated making a preliminary review first. As a result, it was passed and seven members were elected to be responsible. They are currently reviewing it and plan to convene a second joint meeting at 2 p.m. to conduct a thorough discussion before drafting an opinion and submitting it to the general meeting on Friday. Whether there will be any accompanying amendments is still difficult to predict at this time. (2nd Special Telegram)

Salary Vehicle of the 31st Division Robbed by Bandits En Route 4

One Company Commander Killed and One Wounded

Battalion Commander and Merchants Kidnapped

(Hankou) The salary vehicle of the 31st Division was robbed by bandits at Shuanggang Bridge in the Chongpu market area on the 1st. Two company commanders were killed and one wounded, and the battalion commander and more than forty merchants were kidnapped. (2nd Special Telegram)

Legislative Yuan Secretly Discusses Puyi's Usurpation Issue 5

Submitting Recommendations to the Central Political Council

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 49th meeting on the morning of the 2nd, attended by 77 members including Zhu Hezhong and Luo Ding. Sun Ke chaired the meeting, and Liang Hancao was the Secretary-General. A. Reporting Matters: (1) Reading the minutes of the 48th meeting. (2) The Nanjing City's general budget for local ordinary income and expenditure in the 22nd year was submitted to the National Government with instructions to approve its publication and to order the Executive Yuan and Supervisory Yuan to transfer the relevant matters for compliance and to order the Accounting Department to comply. (3) The resolution of the Yuan, requesting the National Government to issue an order to all central agencies that all taxes, levies, and fees collected without legislative procedures and contracts concluded should be submitted to the Yuan for review before the end of April of this year was submitted to the National Government with instructions to comply. (4) The amendment to the Electricity Enterprise Regulations was submitted to the National Government with instructions and has been promulgated and ordered to be implemented. B. Matters for Discussion: The Yuan held a secret meeting on the morning of the 2nd, reportedly to discuss the issue of the puppet organization and Puyi's usurpation, and to suggest counter-measures to the central government. After several hours, other cases were discussed. Due to the passage of time, it was left for the next meeting to discuss. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

(Nanjing) At the 49th meeting of the Legislative Yuan on the morning of the 2nd, after the reading of the reporting matters was completed, member Jiao Yitang stood up and made a temporary motion, stating that Puyi's usurpation and proclamation as emperor required a serious expression from the National Government regarding this rebellious action. Peng Yangguang and others seconded the motion, and President Sun Ke announced a change to a secret meeting, requesting all attendees to leave. The atmosphere in the meeting was quite tense. After discussing until 12 noon, the President summarized everyone's opinions, combined three items, and handed them to the Secretary-General to draft recommendations to be submitted to the Central Political Council. The contents: (1) The National Government should issue a declaration, notifying all countries of the world, reiterating the significance of not recognizing the puppet organization, hoping that the countries would sympathize and unanimously deny it. (2) Prevent domestic traitors from engaging in activities for the puppet organization and establish methods for punishing traitors to be implemented by military and political organs. (3) Overthrowing the Qing Dynasty was the consensus of the people of the whole country. The current actions in the Northeast are carried out under the coercion of the Japanese. The government should issue a statement, explaining the righteousness and proclaiming to the national citizens to unanimously deny the puppet organization. After the meeting, the Secretariat drafted a recommendation letter and submitted it to the Central Political Council for adoption. (2nd Special Telegram)

De Wang Invites Xiao Zhenying to Discuss the Demarcation of Autonomous Regions 6

(Beiping) Zhangjiakou Telegram: De Wang invited Xiao Zhenying to Bailingmiao to discuss the issue of the division of Mongolian autonomous regions. Xiao replied on the 2nd, stating that he was burdened with official duties and requested that De Wang come to Zhangjiakou for nearby consultation. (2nd Telegram)

(Nanjing) De Wang's representatives, Guo Wang and Mongolian committee member Bai Rui, went to Ganzhou to meet with Chiang Kai-shek. On the morning of the 2nd, they returned to Nanjing. According to Bai Rui, Guo Wang plans to meet with the central authorities within days before returning to Mongolia to report to De Wang on the progress of his visit to Beijing. Furthermore, with the Puyi's usurpation and the Japanese and puppet forces aggressively invading Inner Mongolia, it is planned to give De Wang a considerable title to strengthen the border. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) De Wang's representative, Guo Wang, went to Ganzhou to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to request instructions on the Inner Mongolia autonomy plan. On the morning of the 2nd, he arrived in Nanjing by ship from Xun. At 10 a.m., he met with President Wang, accompanied by his secretary Su Yingde, to report on everything. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

Zhangjia Enters Mongolia This Afternoon After Bidding Farewell to All Parties Yesterday 7

(Beiping) Zhangjia is scheduled to enter Mongolia by special train at 1 p.m. on the 3rd. He has already bid farewell to all parties on the 2nd. The travel expenses for this trip are set at 60,000 yuan. His itinerary will first take him to Suiyuan, then to the Yikezhao League, and then to the Tumote Banner, Alashan Banner, U League, and Xilingol League, and finally to the Twelve Banners and Xuanhua in Chahar Province. It is planned to promote popularization in accordance with the Xuanhua outline within five months, and to prepare five kinds of books for the Mongolian people, lamas, princes, and youth, including the Premier's Legacy. Zhang also serves concurrently as a member of the General Staff Headquarters Border Affairs Group to investigate everything. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Zhangjia will change to going to Zhangjiakou at noon on the 3rd, stay briefly, and then transfer to Mongolia to spread enlightenment and inspect the leagues and banners. (2nd Special Telegram)

Tibetan Troops Cross the Tongtian River 8

Start Contacting Sichuan Troops

Liu Wenhui Telegram Reports to Beijing

(Nanjing) The Central Government received a telegram from Zhu Shaoliang, proving that Tibetan troops had secretly crossed the Tongtian River and had begun to contact Sichuan troops. Liu Wenhui telegraphed the Central Government, reporting that Tibetan troops had repeatedly invaded Xikang. He had sent troops to the Tibetan army camp to repeatedly persuade them, but the Tibetan troops had always been deluded and had continued their invasion. They had also spied on the weaknesses of our army and secretly crossed the Tongtian River. The war had begun. He requested that the Tibetan ruling authorities be quickly instructed to strictly stop it in order to maintain peace. (2nd Special Telegram)

Mongolian Tibetan Affairs Commission Holds Regular Meeting 9

(Nanjing) The Mongolian Tibetan Affairs Commission held a regular meeting on the 2nd, chaired by Shi Qingyang. Multiple motions were discussed, and Bai Yunti was elected to attend and report on next week's memorial service. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

Liu Wenlong and Others Declare Preservation of the Integrity of the New Province 10

Eliminate the Disasters Inflicted by Ma Zhongying's Disturbance of the People and Harm to the Country

Please Ask the Central Government to Allocate Funds to Reorganize the Finances of the New Province

(Nanjing) A certain agency received a declaration issued by Liu Wenlong, Sheng Shicai, He Duoniyazi, etc. in Dihua, stating the course of the events in southern Xinjiang and the measures taken to deal with them. It first described Ma Zhongying's troubles in Xinjiang, then stated that Ma wanted to establish a Muslim country, colluded with Zhang Peiyuan, and attempted to overthrow the provincial government. Finally, it claimed that the King of Khotan in southern Xinjiang occupied Kashgar and organized an independent Muslim East Turkestan government, seceding from the Republic of China. The provincial government immediately submitted the news to the provincial affairs conference for discussion. (1) Preserve the entire land and people of Xinjiang. (2) Assist the people against the King of Khotan. (3) Eliminate the disasters inflicted by Ma Zhongying's disturbance of the people and harm to the country. (4) Telegraphed the Central Government requesting an allocation of 5 million yuan in debt to reorganize the finances of the province in order to relieve the suffering of the people of Xinjiang. (2nd Special Telegram)

Current Commentary

The Germanic Empire and Hitler 11

Heng

Historians who discuss European civilization often say that Greece was succeeded by Rome, and Rome was succeeded by the Germanic people. After reading Western history, we are even more convinced of this. When Greece declined, it was conquered by Rome, and its culture was also inherited by Rome. When Rome declined, it was conquered by the Germanic people, and even the name of the empire it had built was inherited by them. The so-called Holy Roman Empire was not really an empire of the Romans but an empire of the Germanic people. Later, the Germanic people also contributed greatly to maintaining Western European civilization by blocking the Huns in Austria, resisting the Turks in the lower Danube, and hindering the westward advance of the Mongols. Looking at the fact that there are still 18 million Germanic people living in various places in continental Europe outside of Germany today, one can imagine the grandeur of the Germanic people's conquests in those days. Therefore, from a historical perspective, the Germanic people are indeed a great nation in Europe with a long-standing reputation. When Napoleon ravaged Germany, the Germanic national spirit was aroused again. After half a century of brewing, under the leadership of Prussia, various states united to create the empire before the Great War. The Germans called this empire the Second Empire, so as to distinguish it from the Holy Roman Empire of the past. The power and splendor of this empire still excites the Germans today. Hitler took advantage of this and called for the creation of the Third Empire, meaning that if the Germanic nation wants to restore its past glory and create future achievements, it must first unite the Germanic people scattered in various places into a large group. His ambition is truly astonishing. Judging from the past history of the Germanic nation, it cannot be said to be a completely empty and extravagant hope.

However, today's international environment is very different from the international environment of the previous two empires. The methods adopted by Hitler are also clumsy and inappropriate. When Charlemagne the Great rose, the Roman Empire was already old and declining, while the Germanic people were strong and good at fighting. The law of the jungle was very easy. Moreover, at that time, there were no strong countries monitoring its side, so it could do whatever it wanted. By the time the Second Empire was established, there were four strong European countries: Russia in the north, Austria in the east, France in the south, and England, which dominated the seas, across the strait to the west. Therefore, there was already more resistance in the international arena. With Bismarck's skillful and flexible diplomatic skills, he was still able to use the international situation at the time to allow this empire to be born safely. When we read the history of that time, we know that Bismarck was able to create a great career because he showed people that he was incapable, so that people did not know that he had the grand ambition of unifying the 38 states of Germany into a great power; he formed many alliances to trap the enemy in isolation; and he challenged people but instead made people bear the name of being the instigator of the war. Therefore, during the Austro-Prussian War, Austria was full of arrogance and was pressing hard. International observers also allowed the Austrians to win, so they all secretly sided with the Prussians. When the Prussians won and became the leader of the Germanic Confederation, they were resented by Napoleon III of France. On the eve of the Franco-Prussian War, the French were arrogant and invincible. Prussia hid its strength in many ways, so that its sharp edge was not revealed. Therefore, England, Russia, and other countries were all worried, Italy even helped Prussia attack France, and Austria also remained neutral. The French lost all sympathy in the international arena. As a result, Prussia directly attacked Paris. After these two wars, the Germanic states united with each other, and the German Empire was formally established. From this point of view, Bismarck's way of winning was to conserve energy and hide his strength internally. The enemy did not realize it and was taken advantage of. Bismarck was deeply aware of the subtleties of the saying "the mournful one wins" in the military.

As for the current Hitler, it is not the same. The environment he is in is even more difficult than before the unification of the Germanic states. After the Great War, people have suffered enough from the terror of German militarism and are heavily guarded. The Germans are bound by the peace treaty and have no colonies to supply raw materials, so it is difficult for them to realize their ambitions. Therefore, for Hitler, it is more appropriate to follow Bismarck's old wisdom of conserving energy and waiting for the opportunity, and to make full use of the contradictions between countries to gain the sympathy of countries other than the hypothetical enemy. However, Hitler does not care about the international situation or the strength of the country. He first shows people a ferocious face and alarming words, so that those who have hatred guard against him even more, and those who have no hatred turn into enemies. Up to today, he has not only incurred the jealousy of the Russians, but also lost the favor of the English. France and the Little Entente are out of the question. Even Austria, which is said to be of the same culture and race, is also at odds with him. In short, it is all caused by his fondness for high-sounding theories and a fierce appearance. If he continues to act willfully, not only will the Third Empire not be established, but he will also create many enemies and put Germany in a situation from which it cannot recover. If Hitler really wants to achieve great things, why not follow Bismarck's policies?

Jiang Dingwen Banquets Senior Guangdong Generals 12

Bandit Suppression Plan Largely Agreed Upon

Eliminate Territorial Boundaries and Establish Genuine Contact

Chairman Chiang Sends Long Telegrams to Chen and Chiang

(Hong Kong) On the 2nd, Jiang Dingwen hosted a banquet for more than a dozen senior generals, including Chen Jitang, Yu Hanmou, and Miao Peinan, at Tuisi Garden. Security was extremely tight, and the banquet lasted three hours before it ended. In addition to discussing bandit suppression, Jiang's visit also aimed to promote unification and invite Guangdong committee members to take positions in Beijing. On the 2nd, Jiang sent his chief secretary Zhang Jiong to meet with reporters, talking about Jiang's continuous discussions on bandit suppression in Guangdong in recent days, and that the first phase of the joint suppression plan has been largely agreed upon. First, the territorial boundaries between Guangdong and Fujian will be eliminated, mutual contact will be established, and bandits on the Fujian-Guangdong border will be eliminated. The Eastern Route Army currently has ten divisions, divided into four columns, with Wei Lihuang serving as the front-line commander. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Hong Kong) Li Zongren's visit to Guangdong is indefinite. Jiang plans to return to Fujian by Guangdong military plane on the 3rd. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Hong Kong) Those who came to Guangdong with Jiang Dingwen also included Lin Weiwen. Jiang and Lin each received a long telegram from Chiang Kai-shek on the morning of the 1st. After discussing it at the political meeting at noon, they jointly replied to Chiang in the evening. Jiang again sent a long telegram to Chen Jitang on the morning of the 2nd. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Guangzhou) Jiang Dingwen continued to hold meetings with Chen Jitang today to discuss the suppression of the Communists. Jiang later told the guests that the Central Army in Fujian now has ten divisions, which will be formed into the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Army. It has now been decided that the Eastern Route Army will be engaged in pacifying northern Fujian, and the Southern Route Army, led by Chen Jitang, will be responsible for suppressing the Communists. The Jiangxi authorities hope to complete the work of exterminating the bandits by the end of May. Wei Lihuang will serve as the front-line commander and set up a headquarters in Xiamen. After today's meeting, Jiang visited the four townships of Guangzhou. (Reuters Telegram, 2nd)

Internal Strife in the Quanzhou-Yongchun People's Army, Hong Wende's Troops Occupy Yongchun City 13

Hong Sends a Telegram to Condemn Zhang, Zhang Xiongnan Retreats to Dehua

The Third Division Concentrates in Zhangzhou and Tong'an, Waiting to Depart for Longyan

Zhang Zhen Flies to Shanghai, Transfers to Ganzhou, Wei Lihuang Arrives in Quanzhou

(Xiamen) Quanzhou Telegram: Internal fighting in the Quanzhou-Yongchun People's Army. Hong Wende's troops occupied Yongchun City on the 28th. The east and west routes have joined, and Zhang Xiongnan has retreated to Dehua. Chen Yucai is pursuing eastward towards Dehua and has sent a telegram to condemn Zhang. Wei Lihuang returned to Quanzhou by car from the provincial capital on the 28th. Xiao Jing, director of the Western District Security Sub-Bureau, arrived in Xiamen by the Haicheng ship from the provincial capital on the morning of the 2nd and is scheduled to go to Quanzhou on the 3rd. Xiao also serves concurrently as the director of the Southern District Security Sub-Bureau. According to the provincial government, the principle of reorganizing the People's Army is that the fewer, the better. The province is currently planning to organize seven regiments. This visit is to verify the actual number, because the reports from various routes are too many. First Xingquan Yong, then Zhang district (2nd Special Telegram)

(Xiamen) Zhang Zhen arrived in Shanghai on the 2nd. A Guangdong plane flew to Shanghai and transferred to Ganzhou to meet Chiang Kai-shek. The 9th Division Li Yannian was transferred to Zhangzhou. The 25th Brigade Supplementary Regiment, Special Forces, with more than 8,000 people, arrived in Zhangzhou at noon on the 2nd. The 26th Brigade can arrive on the 3rd. Li also serves as the commander of the Fourth Column, under the jurisdiction of the 39th and 2nd Divisions. Li arrived in Xiamen from Quanzhou on the 2nd and will go to Zhangzhou on the 3rd. The three divisions are concentrated in Zhangzhou and Tong'an, waiting to depart for Longyan. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Xiamen) Japanese military officer Zuo Fang Fanmu and Taiwan Governor-General's Office sent personnel to Ze Chongxin to conduct commercial and economic surveys in Fujian. They arrived in Zhangzhou on the 2nd to meet with Longxi County Chief and 3rd Division Chief Li Yutang. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Xiamen) Quanzhou News: More than 4,000 people from Hong Wende's troops entered Yongchun. (Fuzhou) Wei Lihuang came to the province to discuss the main points of advancing to suppress the Communist bandits in western Fujian and the post-war pacification of southern Fujian before returning to Quanzhou. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

(Fuzhou) Military news: The bandit suppression in northern Fujian is winning victory after victory. There are no traces of bandits in the entire territory of Yongan. The remnants of bandits in Jiangle are trapped between Fuguzhengfang and can be completely eliminated. (2nd Special Telegram)

Tang Enbo Concurrently Serves as Commander of the Fourth Division 14

(Fuzhou) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek appointed Tang Enbo concurrently as commander of the Fourth Division, and Leng Xin was transferred to chief of staff of the Tenth Column Command. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

Xu Xiangqian's Bandits Encircle Maduguan, Repelled 17

Wang Lingji Flies to Chengdu to Meet Liu Xiang for Instructions

(Chongqing) Xu Xiangqian used all his strength to attack the Fifth Route Army, sending a surprise force to encircle the Maduguan clan chief Hao Yaoyan's troops. Fortunately, the air force flew to their rescue, repelling the bandits and annihilating more than a thousand of them. Liu Xiang increased the dispatch of the entire First Division Chief Tang Shizun to reinforce, Tang has arrived at Kaijiang and is transferring to the front line to supervise the battle. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Chongqing) Wang Lingji flew to Chengdu to meet with Liu Xiang for instructions. (2nd Special Telegram)

Japanese Army Exercises in Southern Tianjin, the Central Government Considers Countermeasures 18

Telegrams Ordered the Beiping Authorities to Make Serious Representations to the Japanese Side

(Nanjing) More than a thousand Japanese troops in North China departed from Tianjin and conducted large-scale joint exercises in the area along the Tianjin-Pukou Railway towards Liangwangzhuang, Tangguantun, and Jinghai. The Hebei Provincial Government's polite refusal was ineffective. Telegrams have been sent to the Central Government, the Beiping Military Sub-Commission, and the Political Consolidation Council for instructions. At the same time, the Railway Ministry also received a report from the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau, requesting instructions on how to deal with the situation. The government believes that this move by the Japanese side not only violates the Boxer Protocol but also disregards our country's sovereignty. It has now telegraphed the Beiping Military and Political Committees, ordering them to make serious representations to the Japanese side and exchange places for exercises to avoid misunderstandings. It is also heard that the Central Government is paying close attention to the recent actions of the Japanese side in North China and is considering countermeasures. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) The Japanese army stationed in Tianjin divided the exercises and marches along the Tianjin-Pukou Line into two major groups. The first group was designated as the Southern Army and bivouacked in Tangguantun and Jinghai. The second group was designated as the Northern Army and bivouacked in Liangwangzhuang. Commander Nakamura of the military headquarters personally went to review them. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway Station offices in the area were mostly temporarily occupied by the Japanese army. On the 3rd, there was a scrimmage exercise, and on the morning of the 4th, the final exercise was held at the Guandi Temple in Gedacun, a southwestern suburb of Tianjin. In the morning, they returned to the Japanese barracks in Haiguang Temple. It was found that the area of this exercise by the Japanese army fundamentally violated the Boxer Protocol. Their strong demand for vehicles from Tianjin-Pukou and their self-designated name as the "Japanese Road Protection Team" are particularly inappropriate. (Central News Agency Telegram, 2nd)

There Are Still Problems with the Reception of the Passes of the Great Wall 19

The Japanese Side Uses Pretexts to Not Withdraw Troops

The Authorities Ordered Yin Tao to Negotiate

(Tianjin) There are still problems with the reception of the passes of the Great Wall. The Japanese side has stationed 400 troops in Shaheqiao, 600 in Shimenzhai, and 300 in Malanyu, using the excuse that there are no houses outside the Great Wall to not withdraw. The authorities ordered Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming to negotiate separately on this matter. (2nd Special Telegram)

Yin Rugeng Has Returned to Ping from Tongxian 20

Today to Go to Gubeikou to Handle Reception

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng returned to Ping from Tongxian last night. It is scheduled to go to Gubeikou at 8:00 AM on the 3rd to handle the reception. According to reports, of the five small passes affiliated with Gubeikou, such as Baimaguan and Dashuiyu, only Paizilu and Liangko still have a small number of Japanese troops, while the rest have already withdrawn. When we take over, we will immediately dispatch security teams for defense. It is incorrect to say that the pseudo-customs at various passes of the Great Wall have increased import and export duties since yesterday. Moreover, the Japanese side has already withdrawn to outside the passes when the pseudo-customs are handed over to each pass. In the future, after a negotiated solution, they can also be cancelled. (2nd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng is scheduled to go to Gubeikou again early on the 2nd to handle the reception. On the 2nd, Yin telegraphed Yu Xuezhong, reporting that the Japanese 7th and 8th Divisions at Gubeikou had completed their rotation of troops and that the reception could be implemented before noon on the 4th. (2nd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong said that the bandits in Qian'an and Zunhua have been pacified and the local area is safe. It is not easy to administer the counties east of Wan. The county magistrates cannot actively proceed because of special circumstances, and it is easy to offend people. If power is eliminated, then the traitors will collude and foreign aid will run rampant, so it is necessary to move and change the county magistrates to avoid unscrupulous attacks. (2nd Dispatch)

Hand Grenade Explosion Near Hai Guang Temple in Tianjin 32

(Tianjin) At 12:00 AM on the 1st, a loud hand grenade explosion was heard outside the north wall of the Japanese barracks at Haiguang Temple in Xiguan, Tianjin. Police from the 2nd Precinct of the 6th District went to investigate, but the person who threw the grenade was nowhere to be found. There was a copper basin hat, two severed fingers, and grenade fragments on the ground. Nearby rickshaw pullers reported that the person who threw the grenade seemed to have been injured, looked like a worker, and had escaped into a certain concession by rickshaw. After the bomb exploded, no one came out of the Japanese barracks, as if they had not heard anything. (2nd Dispatch)

Tianjin Yuyuan Factory Closes Down 33

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Yuyuan Yarn Factory closed down on the 2nd, leaving more than 4,000 male and female workers unemployed. It lost millions of dollars in business last year. Recently, the board of directors decided to suspend work. There are a total of six yarn factories in Tianjin, one run by the Japanese and five run by the Chinese. Since the Beiyang Wanyuan and today's Yuyuan factories have suspended work, only two remain, and they are also showing signs of being unsustainable. (2nd Dispatch)

British House of Commons Discusses the Question of Pseudo-Organization and Simon's Reply 56

No Reports Received from Countries Other Than Japan Wanting to Recognize It

League of Nations to Convene Advisory Committee to Study Pseudo-Postal Issues

(London) Today, Changchun is holding a celebration for Puyi's usurpation of the throne, and the House of Commons is also discussing the "Manchukuo" issue. A question was asked to Foreign Secretary Simon regarding which countries, other than Japan, want to recognize "Manchukuo." Foreign Secretary Simon replied that he had not received any reports of any countries wanting to recognize "Manchukuo." This question was raised by Conservative MP Post. (1st Reuters Dispatch)

(Changchun) General Ryo Hishikari, the ambassador stationed in "Manchukuo," and Prime Minister Zheng Xiaoxu of the puppet government exchanged official documents regarding the establishment of the "Manchu Empire" at 3:00 PM yesterday. The document submitted by Zheng Xiaoxu to Ambassador Hishikari stated that "Manchukuo" had established a constitutional monarchy today and hoped that this intention would be conveyed to the government of your country. The document submitted by Ambassador Hishikari to Zheng Xiaoxu stated that the Japanese government had notified this ambassador of the intention to acknowledge the notification. This ambassador has the honor of replying based on this instruction. (2nd Dentong Dispatch)

(London) On February 16th of this year, the British government notified the Secretary-General of the League of Nations that the London Post Office had received a letter from the Postal Administration of "Manchukuo" requesting that various statistical tables be sent to "Manchukuo" in accordance with the provisions of the Postal Union Convention in order to settle the postage for mail sent to and from Manzhou via transit. The British government is very willing to know to what extent foreign post offices have a factual relationship with the "Manchukuo" post office without giving the impression of recognizing the existing organization of Manzhou. After receiving the notification, Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, decided to convene the advisory committee organized by the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly on February 24, 1933, in order to study methods that would enable the postal regulations to be implemented between various countries and Manzhou on the one hand, and not give the impression that various countries recognize "Manchukuo" on the other. It is heard that this advisory committee will be held in Geneva in the near future for discussion. (1st Havas Dispatch)

The Manchester Guardian Comments on Puyi's Usurpation of the Throne 57

Said to be a Sharply Pointed Blade Flashing from Tokyo

The Times Actually Speaks for Japan

(London) The Manchester Guardian commented on Puyi's assumption of the throne today, saying, "If 'Manchukuo' exists and has an emperor, then violence has led to it. The organizational laws limit Puyi's various powers and place jurisdiction in the hands of Japanese advisors. Those who maintain the paradise of 'Manchukuo' and expand it are sharply pointed blades flashing from Tokyo." (2nd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Most newspapers today also commented on Puyi's usurpation of the throne in lengthy articles. The Times expressed sympathy for Puyi and praised his achievements, vaguely saying, "'Puyi declared that since taking office as the chief executive, he has done his best to eliminate international shocks and eliminate the ravages of warlords and bandits for the people, so that they can live and work in peace, and he has also unified the currency to stabilize it,' which is still reasonable. Although the new organization in Manzhou has no other achievements, if it can reform the currency system, it has benefited the local area a lot. Moreover, it can punish bandits, improve transportation, and turn a corner of Changchun into a modern city. In short, no matter how 'Manchukuo' originated, we cannot but express our admiration for the spirit of its organization and its firm will. Countries with commercial relations in the Far East have all expressed satisfaction with 'Manchukuo's' willingness to respect the principle of open doors. These countries must decide how their businesses can operate in 'Manchukuo' without hindering the League of Nations' principle of 'non-recognition of Manchukuo.' It is not too late to act." Journalist Patrick expressed his opinion in the News Chronicle, saying, "Puyi changed his title to Emperor Kangde. The word 'De' is indeed worthy of it. As for the word 'Kang', judging from the current situation, I am afraid that I cannot be so optimistic, because the danger of war is not as great as last autumn, but it still exists." Lord Clive published an article in the Morning Post, describing what he saw during his travels in "Manchukuo" and recording his conversation with Puyi in May 1933. He concluded that he believed that the future of "Manchukuo" would be peaceful and would not lead to war. "'Puyi has a long period of experience and is not lacking in experience. When the time comes, he will move forward bravely, because he believes that it is his duty.'" (2nd Havas)

Special Disarmament Conference to be Convened in London at the End of this Month 59

The United States Proposes the Conclusion of a World Non-Aggression Pact

Armaments May Not Be Used to Invade Neighboring Countries

Nine Countries Have Been Invited to Participate in the Conference

(London) The British government has now scheduled a special disarmament conference to be convened in London at the end of this month. According to sources, this conference will be the most important disarmament conference in recent years. The United States will put forward an astonishing proposal to conclude a worldwide non-aggression treaty, which is compared to President Roosevelt's plan. It is heard that in addition to limiting or abolishing offensive weapons, it must also be guaranteed that the remaining armaments cannot be used to invade neighboring countries. The countries invited to participate in this special conference are the United States, France, Italy, Germany, Russia, Japan, Poland, Belgium, and Spain. The Little Entente countries (i.e., Romania, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia) will also be invited. According to Simon and Henderson's opinions, if Eden's report is well received, then this special conference can at least negotiate a settlement based on the British-Italian memorandum. (2nd National Telegram)

(London) Well-informed circles in London do not admit the claim that Britain is making a final effort on disarmament, but non-political circles feel that the opportunity to conclude a disarmament convention will depend on whether Lord Privy Seal Eden's report is acceptable. Eden had previously gone to Paris, Rome, and Berlin to explain the British disarmament memorandum and seek to form the backbone of a disarmament convention. He returned to London from the European continent tonight. When Eden arrived, a Reuters representative went to see him. Eden said that the trip was very beneficial and had removed certain difficulties and misunderstandings. The opinions of the two governments (Germany and Italy) on the British disarmament memorandum have been clearly understood. He believes that the opinions of the third government (France) will also be known soon, so his mission on this trip is completed, and this time he has the opportunity to meet with major European politicians, which is very beneficial.

Reuters has learned that the British government is preparing to deliberate on the revision of the British plan, but it is believed that if the British plan is not accepted by all countries, then no country can temporarily propose another plan to replace it. At the same time, London is optimistic that Eden's trip has brought the conclusion of the convention closer. The British Cabinet will decide on a policy based on Eden's report within a few days, which may have a good impact on the overall situation of world disarmament.

The attitude of the United States towards Eden's report is very important, and President Roosevelt's special envoy, Davis, happened to arrive in London tonight, which is very noteworthy. Davis will meet with Eden to discuss everything.

Before leaving Paris to return to his country today, Eden had several hours of consultation with French Prime Minister Doumergue and French Foreign Minister Barthou. At the end of the meeting, Barthou greatly admired Eden's talent, saying that Eden had an exciting and outstanding will. This kind of off-topic statement cannot eliminate the pessimism held by Paris that the future of the convention has not been greatly brightened by Eden's trip.

When Eden left the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the French authorities issued a communiqué stating that Eden had reported to Doumergue and Barthou on his talks in Berlin and Rome and explained the principles of the British memorandum based on this information. Doumergue and Barthou then informed Eden that they would continue to study and notify the French government's decision within days.

When Eden left the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs, he only said, "We have done a little good work."

(1st Reuters Dispatch)

The reasons for the postponement of the reception of Gubeikou are related to the usurpation of the title by Pu Ni. On-the-spot inspection of Gubeikou. Beiping correspondence, the reception of Gubeikou was originally scheduled for February 28, but due to various reasons, it was changed to March 4. The reporter went to Gubeikou by car from Ping on February 27 to conduct an on-the-spot inspection. The information obtained is recorded as follows: For this reception of Gubeikou, our side had already completed all the procedures. In advance, Yin Rugeng, the commissioner in charge of the reception, and the Japanese side agreed on a plan to receive it on the 28th. Representatives from both sides met in Gubeikou on the 26th to prepare all the procedures. Liu Youxun, the newly appointed Director of the Gubeikou Zazhi Bureau on our side, Huo Shi, the Director of the Gubeikou Office of the Jiji Administrative Commissioner's Office, and Guan Qinghua, the Director of the Gubeikou Public Security Bureau, arrived in Miyun in advance to prepare everything. Yin Rugeng set off from Ping on the 25th. When passing through Miyun, he accompanied Huo Shi, Liu Youxun, Guan Qinghua, etc. to Gubeikou. He only arrived at 4 pm that afternoon and temporarily prepared the Japanese military club in Hebei as a temporary office. That evening, he met with Nagami Toshihide, the commander of the 25th Regiment of the 7th Division of the Japanese Army stationed in Gubeikou and the commander of the Gubeikou garrison. On the 26th, Matsui, the Japanese commissioner, also arrived in Gubeikou from Chengde to discuss all the handover procedures with Yin. Due to various reasons, it was decided to postpone the reception to March 4. On the 27th, another discussion was held to confirm everything. The main points agreed upon were roughly as follows: (1) The administrative and police affairs of Gubeikou will be completely taken over by our side; (2) The Japanese army and its affiliated organs will be moved out as soon as the houses outside the pass are built; (3) All organs set up by the puppet state in Gubeikou must be removed. However, because there are no houses outside the pass, they will be temporarily moved to the foot of the Great Wall; (4) The inspection posts set up by the puppet government at Nantianmen, Beixiagang and Gubeikou Shangpo should be removed immediately; (5) The reception will be carried out on March 4; (6) The personnel in charge of the handover from both sides will arrive in Gubeikou on the 3rd, and the reception ceremony will be held on the morning of the 4th. After Matsui agreed on all the issues, he returned to Chengde at 2 pm on the 27th. There are three reasons for the postponement of the reception: (1) Pu Ni usurped the title on March 1. The Japanese and puppet forces in Gubeikou forced the people to hold a large-scale celebration. If we were to receive it at this time and prohibit it, it would not be allowed in fact. It would be inconvenient to sit idly by; (2) Most of the public houses and larger houses in Gubeikou were occupied by the Japanese and puppet organs. Although the puppet organs decided to withdraw, it would take time to move. In addition, they were preparing to celebrate Pu Ni's usurpation of the title and had not yet moved, so our organs did not have suitable houses for office; (3) The Japanese army stationed in the entire territory of Rehe was originally a part of the Nishigi Regiment of the 1st Division. The Gubeikou area was garrisoned by the Hayakawa Unit of the 31st Regiment of the Regiment. The Japanese side considered that the unit had been stationed outside for a long time and was due to be replaced. In mid-February, the main regiment transferred the Sugihara Daitaro Unit of the 7th Division to take over, and transferred the 8th Division back to the main regiment. During the period of troop deployment and handover, there were many twists and turns in the handover of military and political affairs. The reception of Gubeikou happened at this time and would be affected. Due to these various reasons, both sides agreed to reschedule to allow sufficient time to prepare calmly. After both sides decided to reschedule the reception on the 26th, Yin Rugeng immediately drafted a telegram and asked the Japanese side to forward it to Beiping to report the process and notify the remaining reception personnel to postpone their trip. However, the telegram was not forwarded by the Japanese Embassy's Takegimiya Shibayama until 12 pm on the 27th. Therefore, Qiu Heting, the magistrate of Miyun County, and Xu Shiying, the commander of the Second Battalion of the Second Security Regiment of the war zone, etc., all rushed to Gubeikou on the afternoon of the 27th because they had not heard of it. Thirty-one policemen who were to be received also drove from Miyun to Shixia on the same day. Yin considered that it would be inconvenient to live in Gubeikou since the reception had been postponed, so he left Gubeikou at 7 am on the 28th with Liu Youxun, Huo Shi, Qiu Heting, Xu Shiying, Guan Qinghua and Xu Qing'en, leaving only one or two staff members to guard the houses there. The police were temporarily ordered to wait for orders in Shixia. Yin and others arrived in Shixia at about 9 am, summoned the police for a lecture and gave some instructions. They arrived in Miyun at about 10 am, had lunch at the county office, and Qiu Heting, the magistrate of Miyun County, and Xu Shiying, the commander of the Second Security Battalion, returned to the office. Yin and others returned directly to Beiping and decided to go to the reception again on the 4th. The Japanese representative is also expected to arrive on the same day. The reception on the 4th is expected to not cause any more problems. Of the five small passes near Gubeikou, the three passes to the west are Baimaguan, Shitanglu and Dazishuiyu. The Japanese army has mostly withdrawn and there is no problem with the reception. The two small passes to the east are Caojialu and Qiangzilou. These two passes are adjacent to Rehe and bandits often sneak into the pass through them, disturbing the people in the war zone. The situation is extremely serious. Now, Japanese and puppet troops are stationed there. After the reception of Gubeikou, negotiations will be held with the Japanese side, and our side will send security teams to station there to eliminate the source of the chaos. The reception of Malanyu has also been recognized by the Japanese side. The Japanese army currently stationed in the Gubeikou area is the Nagami Toshihide Unit of the 25th Regiment of the 7th Division, with about 200 soldiers. The regimental headquarters is located in Hebei. A detachment of Japanese military police is stationed there, with about eight or nine soldiers, led by the detachment commander Ogawa. The detachment headquarters is located in Hedong. A branch of the Japanese News Agency is located in Xiaxiagang to handle propaganda matters. It is the only propaganda organ of the Japanese puppet regime in Gubeikou. The Rehe Sakata Transport Office is a commercial transport organ under the protection of the Japanese army and also has an office in Gubeikou, with more than 20 trucks, which transports various contraband and other goods. There are many puppet organs, including (1) the Gubeikou Office of the Rehe Provincial Government, which handles all local administrative affairs, located in Xiapo, headed by Lv Junfu, with about 20 people working there; (2) the Manchukuo Border Police Team, headed by Hong Lu, with 80 puppet police, of whom Japanese account for one-third and Koreans also account for one-third; (3) the Rehe Provincial Transport Anti-Smuggling Team, with about 20 members, who handle the transport and monopoly of contraband such as opium and morphine; (4) the Manchukuo Gubeikou Customs Collection Office, located in Qiaotou, which collects taxes on incoming and outgoing goods; (5) the Manchukuo Post Office Gubeikou Branch, located in Beijie. In addition, the organs set up by the local people under the coercion of the Japanese puppet regime include the Local Maintenance Association and the Defense Regiment. The Japanese army claimed that there were no suitable barracks outside the pass and would not withdraw for the time being. Although the Japanese side agreed to abolish the puppet organs, there were no active preparations. At the same time, the general Han traitors were very active during this period of handover and tried to obstruct it. However, the Rehe Provincial Government Office stopped receiving people's petitions from the 27th, indicating that it was concluding its work. The local population was about 5,000 before the war, but now there are only about 3,000, and most of the rest have fled and have not yet returned. The general people are quite excited to hear that they will be received. After Yin and others arrived in Gubeikou, they held lantern parades and sang Yangko on the 26th and 27th to show their welcome, which proves that the people's hearts have not forgotten their homeland. Since the Japanese army was transferred and preparing for the reception, Gubeikou has tightened martial law. From 8 pm every night, traffic is prohibited, and Japanese and puppet soldiers and police are stationed at Nantianmen, Beixiagang, and Gubeikou Nanguan to strictly check. Passengers must be searched before being released. Those traveling by car must have a Japanese pass before they can pass. Anyone who is slightly suspicious will be detained. On March 1, Puyi claimed the throne, and the Japanese and puppet forces in Gubeikou prepared to hold a large-scale celebration, ordering shops and residents to hang Japanese and puppet flags and to build colorful arches at the intersections of various streets, which were grotesque and unbearable to look at. From Daxiaoxinkailing to Gubeikou, the traces of war still remain along the way, with iron nets discarded on the roadside and the remains of trenches still remaining. The broken walls and ruins bombed by airplanes and artillery are everywhere, which shows the intensity of the war that day. Nantianmen stands high on the top of the mountain, with a majestic terrain and a general demeanor of "one man guards the pass and ten thousand men cannot open it". During the Great Wall Battle, the Japanese army attacked for a long time without success. Later, they invaded from Badaolouzi, and the natural barrier was lost. After the war, the Japanese erected a monument in Gubeikou Nanguan, "The Brave Warriors of the Republic of China Who Died in the War." When we passed by to pay our respects, we felt infinite emotion. The beautiful mountains and rivers have fallen into the hands of the enemy for almost a year. Although it is hoped that they will be received in the future, whether the exercise of local political power will be free when Japanese and puppet forces are mixed is still a big question. (March 1) Jiang Dingwen's situation when passing through Xiamen and arriving in Guangdong —Following the order of Chairman Jiang to discuss the suppression of bandits— —Chen Jitang hosted a banquet for Jiang that evening— Xiamen correspondence, the Red bandits in Jiangxi Province retreated to the southeast of Jiangxi when the Central Army entered Fujian. The Central Army, in addition to using a large army to suppress and prevent their spread, temporarily suspended the suppression. When the military affairs of Fujian Province were resolved, the Red bandits came out again to disturb the areas of Jiangle and Shaxian. However, the Red bandits had become the end of a powerful crossbow. After fierce battles for more than ten days, they were unable to break through. Chairman Jiang has now decided to unite with four armies to launch a large-scale encirclement and suppression. Jiang Dingwen, the Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression, was ordered to go to Guangdong to discuss the joint suppression with Chen Jitang. After receiving the order, Jiang first sent Chen Zhuokan, the Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, Hong Chao, the Adjutant, and a telegraph operator to Guangdong on February 18 to make contact in advance. At that time, it was reported here that Jiang Dingwen had personally gone to Guangdong, which was the reason. Jiang originally planned to fly to Guangdong on the 23rd, but he telegraphed Nanchang to transfer four Sikorsky aircraft to Fujian for the trip. However, due to continuous rain, the aircraft could not come. On the 27th, the Shanghai-Guangdong flight flew to Guangdong. Jiang took the flight with Zhao Nan, the Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, Zhang Jiong, the Secretary-General, and Lin Weiwen, the Director of the Headquarters. At 12:15 pm on the 27th, he arrived in Xiamen from Fuzhou. The aircraft landed on the sea off Monkey Island near Gulangyu. Liu Guangqian, the Director of the Siming City Preparatory Office, Sun Xiangfu, the Counselor of the Military Affairs Commission, Zhai, a Senior Staff Officer of the Headquarters, and Qi, the Deputy Director of the Adjutant Office, etc. went to greet him. After Jiang got off the aircraft, he rested briefly at the Daqian Hotel by the sea, and then gave a speech to reporters from various newspapers, saying that the mission to Guangzhou was to follow the telegraph order of Chairman Chiang to discuss military affairs for the suppression of bandits with Commander-in-Chief Chen. In the past, the bandit suppression in Jiangxi Province was always tight on the northern and western routes, but lax on the eastern route, and it was also necessary to strengthen the southern route. After the Fujian Rebellion was quelled, Chairman Chiang paid great attention to the bandit suppression on the eastern and southern routes. Therefore, the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Army was established in Fujian Province, with his brother as the Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Route. From now on, the northeastern and western routes can be connected and coordinated. His brother went to Guangdong to discuss the connection between the southeastern and western routes and the bandit suppression strategy with Commander-in-Chief Chen, hoping to achieve the effect of a four-way encirclement. He would return to Guangdong in three to five days to begin supervising the suppression. The Eastern Route Headquarters would be moved to Zhangzhou or Longyan depending on the needs of the military progress on the front line, etc. Jiang did not meet with representatives of various social groups, and then took the Shanghai-Guangdong aircraft to Guangdong at 1:15 pm. (February 28) Guangzhou correspondence, Jiang Dingwen arrived in Guangzhou from Xiamen on the Guangdong-Shanghai Civil Aviation aircraft on February 27. After Chen Jitang received the news, he immediately sent Zeng Qiang, the Director of the Adjutant Office, and Luo Guangqian, the Section Chief, etc., to take a motor boat to the Nantoushi Airport to greet him that afternoon. At 4:30 pm, the aircraft arrived at the Nantoushi Airport. After Jiang got off the aircraft, he shook hands with the welcomers as a courtesy, and then took the motor boat prepared by the First Army Group Headquarters to the Tianzi Pier to land. At 6 pm, Chen hosted a banquet at Tuisi Garden in Dongshan to welcome Jiang, and invited Zou Lu, Deng Zhiru, Chen Rong, Liu Jiwen and other members of the Southwest Political Affairs Council to accompany him. During the banquet, Jiang described in detail the process of suppressing the Fujian Rebellion, and also discussed the future suppression of bandits. Recently, the Fujian situation has been quelled, and he came to Guangdong to meet Commander-in-Chief Chen to discuss the future suppression of bandits. Only two adjutants came with him. The security of Fujian Province has gradually been restored, and the reorganization work has been largely completed. Now, the work of searching for and suppressing the remnants of bandits is underway, etc. (February 28) Progress in the suppression of bandits in Fujian Province Leng and Lu's divisions recover Shaxian Sun's division is also approaching Jiangle The bandits in eastern Fujian are also planning for joint suppression Fuzhou correspondence, the various armies suppressing bandits in northern Fujian have now been formed into the Ninth and Tenth Columns, commanded by Liu Heding and Tang Sibo respectively, and launched a general offensive against the remnants of bandits in Shayong and other places. The military progress has been very rapid in recent days. The bandits west of Yangkou first came into contact with Sun Yuanliang's division. The bandits were defeated and fled to Jiangle, Yong'an and Shaxian. On the 25th, Leng Xin, Lu Xingbang and other divisions took advantage of the victory to attack the bandit troops of the Pseudo Third Army Group in Shaxian. The bandits first used hundreds of youth troops to charge, and the bandit suppression army used machine guns to sweep. The bandits collapsed again. At noon on the 25th, the vanguard of Leng's division and the Tong Yonghan Brigade of Lu's division entered Shaxian County from the southeast and east gates. When they arrived at the Langkou Gutian area, ten miles away from the city, they encountered more than a thousand bandits, and the fierce battle was quite fierce. As a result, the bandits scattered and collapsed outside the city, and then gathered in the Xiamao area (the border between Shunchang and Shaxian). They were again severely attacked by the 246 Brigade of Sun Yuanliang's division. More than a thousand bandits were killed or wounded, and they fled to the western area of Jiangle County in a panic. As a result, Shaxian County was completely recovered. Leng's division was still ordered to join Sun's division to closely follow the bandits and advance towards Yong'an and Jiangle counties. Lu's division was responsible for the defense of Shaxian. According to military sources here, the vanguard of Sun and Leng's divisions had arrived in Yongjiang on the 26th. There were more than a thousand bandits in the area, who were the remnants of bandits from Shaxian, Shunchang and Youxi. They gathered there. Another unit was the bandit masses of the Pseudo First Army Group and Fang Zhimin and Luo Binghui's troops led by Zhu De, totaling about several thousand. They still intended to resist stubbornly by relying on the dangers. Fierce battles took place in Jiangle on the 26th and 27th. There were also minor contacts in Yong'an. According to another report, after Chairman Chiang received Sun Yuanliang's telegram on the 26th reporting the suppression of the Red bandits in Shajiang, he ordered the division to recover Jiangle County within three days. Sun then went to the front line to supervise the battle on the 27th. The important passes of Jiangle, such as Gaotan and Shuinan, have been captured by the 264 Brigade on the 27th. The brigade can advance to Jiangcheng on the 28th. As for the western Fujian area, the various armies suppressing bandits have established contact with the various armies in northern Fujian, and the vanguard has advanced towards Changting. It is reported that Wei Lihuang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Front, will go to Longyan to establish the Front Headquarters. Liu Kan, Li Yannian, Li Yutang and other divisions led by Wei have all arrived at their designated locations, waiting for orders to launch a general offensive against the bandit areas in western Fujian. It is also reported that since the start of the general offensive in the bandit suppression in Fujian Province, the war has progressed very rapidly. Now, Shunchang and Shaxian counties have been recovered by Sun Yuanliang and Leng Xin's divisions respectively. The remnant bandits and the Pseudo Third Army Group retreated to Jiangle and Yong'an. The commanders of Sun and Leng's divisions telegraphed the Fuzhou Headquarters to report the victory, and requested that salt and rice be transported to the bandit areas to provide relief to the refugees. They also led their troops to pursue Jiangle and Yong'an. According to a telegram from Commander Sun yesterday, the remnant bandits were fleeing along the way, and the important passes of Gaotan and Shuinan have been captured one after another. They will be stationed in Jiangcheng today or tomorrow. It is now reported that the Red bandits of the Pseudo 3579 Army Group, who are entrenched on the border between Jiangxi and Jiangxi, know that they cannot resist the large army groups from northern Fujian, western Fujian, and eastern Jiangxi. They have decided to shorten the defense line and guard the counties of Changting, Ninghua, Jianning, Taining, Ruijin, Shicheng, Gengchang, and Lichuan, which are located on the border between Fujian and Jiangxi, as a last struggle. According to intelligence reports, the bandits in Jiangyongmingqing and four other counties have moved their baggage to the rear and forcibly recruited young men to serve as Red soldiers. They seem to be making a general retreat. It is expected that the main forces of both sides will come into contact in the border counties between Fujian and Jiangxi. As for the coastal counties in eastern Fujian, such as Fuding, Xiapu, Fu'an, Ningde, Luoyuan, Lianjiang, Pingtan, etc., local Red troops are rampant. Among them, the troops of Fan Tiemin, Gao Chengxue, etc. (i.e., the Left Wing Vanguard who were organized by Qiu Zhaochen, the Commander of the Eastern Fujian Garrison, during the Pseudo People's Government period to harass Taishun and Pingyang on the border of Zhejiang) adopted guerrilla tactics, colluding with pirates. They usually harass villages and villages along the coast and specialize in looting salt and millet, which they distribute to farmers and fishermen to lure them into joining the army. Once the army comes to suppress them, they flee into the sea. As a result, their party members are increasing day by day, and the local area is suffering unspeakably. They urgently need joint suppression by the sea and land forces to be cleared. It is reported that the Fuzhou Headquarters is planning a joint suppression method with the Majiang Naval Port Command. At the same time, the Provincial Government also intends to order the Maritime Public Security Bureau to plan to restore the water police outposts on the coastal islands and set up police ships to specialize in capturing these Red pirates. (February 28) Zhang Xueliang takes office as Deputy Commander of Bandit Suppression in Hubei Zhang swears to defend the country Hankou correspondence, Zhang Xueliang, the Deputy Commander of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei and Anhui, held an oath-taking ceremony at the headquarters in Wuchang at 9 am on the 1st. Zhang Qun was sent by the Central Government, Xia Douyin was sent by the National Government, and He Chengjun was sent by the Military Affairs Commission to serve as the oath-taking representatives. Those who attended the ceremony included Xu Yuanquan, He Zhuguo, Sun Lianzhong, Shangguan Yunxiang, Rong Jingfang, Ye Peng, Zeng Yiding, Meng Guangpeng, Jia Shiyi, Li Fanyi, Cheng Qibao, Li Shucheng, Lu Zhu, Fan Xiji, Wu Guozhen, Zhou Zechun, Fang Benren, etc. The guard inside and outside the auditorium was strict. The meeting was opened at 9 am, and Zhang Qun presided over the meeting. After the ceremony was performed, Zhang Xueliang raised his hand to take the oath. The oath read, "I solemnly swear that I will恪遵守遵守 Sun Yat-sen's will, implement the Three People's Principles, obey Hu Guan's orders, defend the country, love the people, and fulfill the duties of a soldier. If I violate the oath, I am willing to accept severe punishment." After the oath, Zhang Qun, the oath-taking representative of the Central Government, gave a speech, saying that Deputy Commander Zhang had shared weal and woe with the Party and the country in the past. Last year, he left the country to travel to Europe and had a deep understanding of politics, military affairs, economics, and various facilities. Since returning to the country, he has been more relied upon by the Central Government, and Deputy Commander Zhang will surely make better contributions. Last month, President Wang and Chairman Chiang jointly issued a declaration that the great plan to save the country should be based on suppressing bandits to treat the symptoms and engaging in production and construction. Deputy Commander Zhang is wise and capable and will be able to implement it responsibly to live up to the trust of the Party and the country and to comfort the people's hopes. Next, Xia Douyin, the oath-taking representative of the National Government, gave a speech, saying that the three provinces of Henan, Hubei and Anhui have been suffering from banditry for a long time. Under the personal supervision of Chairman Chiang, 70 to 80% of the bandits have been eliminated. Deputy Commander Zhang has been ordered by the Central Government to come to Hubei to preside over the matter and will surely eliminate the remnants and complete the mission. Deputy Commander Zhang has just returned from overseas and knows that the strength of various countries lies in obeying the leader and being loyal to their duties. I hope that he will assist Chairman Chiang, influence the masses, unify their will, save the country and survive. It depends on this. Next, He Chengjun, the representative of Chairman Chiang, gave a speech, saying that the three provinces of Henan, Hubei and Anhui are located in the center of the country. After the flood, the scars have not yet healed, and the remnants of bandits are also waiting to be eliminated. Deputy Commander Zhang is entrusted with this important task and can implement what he has learned from his European tour in the three provinces first. However, Hubei has always felt that there are many talkers and few doers. I hope that from today onwards, they will understand each other, work together harmoniously, and work together under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, following Deputy Commander Zhang and fulfilling their respective duties and striving to move forward. Finally, Zhang Xueliang replied, saying that his brother's knowledge is shallow and his experience is not deep, but since he has been ordered to come, he can only work hard with his conscience and blood, following the unwavering spirit of Commander-in-Chief Chiang, and implement the plans that Commander-in-Chief Chiang has set. He also hopes that the military and political colleagues in the three provinces will encourage each other. After the ceremony was completed, the meeting was dismissed. On the same day, Zhang Xueliang telegraphed the Central Government, the National Government, the Military Affairs Commission, and the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters, reporting the oath-taking ceremony. At the same time, he telegraphed all parties and separately ordered his subordinates to be informed. Zhang has received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, acting as the commander-in-chief and presiding over the bandit suppression military affairs in the three provinces. He has decided to move into the Wuchang Headquarters within a few days and be stationed for office. The Hankou Administrative Office will be abolished and an office will still be set up. The date of Zhang's visit to Chiang in Jiangxi has not yet been determined. He Zhuguo and others who came to Hankou for instructions will return to their defenses separately on the 2nd. Fourth Aviation Lottery Drawing: Winner of the First Prize at Yi Tai Motors; Winning Tickets Can Be Cashed Starting on the 10th of This Month; Fifth Issue Already Released, Drawing on the 27th of Next Month. The Fourth Issue of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was drawn yesterday at 2 p.m. at Yierbei Road's Yiyuan. Representatives from all sectors were present to supervise. The first prize was won by Yi Tai Motors, sold by the Shanghai Dayun General Company's branch. All winning prizes can be cashed starting from the 10th of this month at the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various locations. The fifth issue was released yesterday. Details are as follows: Venue Arrangement: Yesterday, a banner reading "Aviation Lottery Drawing of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Welcomes All Sectors to Visit" was hung high above the entrance of Yiyuan. To the south was a notice from Director Zheng Lai of the Office regarding scheduled payment dates. A temporary drawing platform was erected, with a banner above reading "The Fourth Issue of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Drawing is Held Here." 甲, 乙, and 丙 machines were placed on the platform. To the west were offices for the Office's staff. To the east were seats for Dayun Company and various agency representatives. A loudspeaker was set up in the center of the venue. French Concession police dispatched both Chinese and Western detectives to provide strict security and maintain order around the platform and the venue. White Russian Yao Kesutuo, residing in Shanghai, rented a large building at No. 1, Lane 1475, Avenue Haig, and opened a roulette gambling den, profiting from the rake-off. The police authorities discovered this and dispatched detectives to investigate the vicinity of the den secretly every night. After confirming the facts, they reported to the First Special District Court, which issued an arrest warrant. Yao was arrested on Broadway Road on Monday of the previous week, and evidence such as chips was seized from the gambling den. He was then handed over to the court for investigation. Because the defendant tried to avoid the jurisdiction of our country's courts, he insisted that he was a Brazilian national. Judge Wu Xiangzu ordered the defendant to be detained pending verification of the facts, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu opened the court and ordered the defendant to be brought in for continued trial. Police lawyers Ru Bao Yi and Qian Xun Jiu, and defendant's lawyer Chen Tan, appeared in court successively. First, White Russian Yipafu from the Russian Relief Society, called as a witness by the police, testified that the defendant was registered as a White Russian in the society in 1901. Next, police officer Lei Di Nuofu testified that he investigated the defendant's registration at the Shanghai Municipal Police Foreign Residents Registration Office and found that the defendant had registered there on February 18, 1929, also declaring himself to be a White Russian, and that his birthplace was indeed in Russia. Lawyer Ru then submitted the defendant's application to the Shanghai Diplomatic Commissioner's Office on June 23, 1926, to register as a Russian resident, in order to prove that the defendant was indeed a White Russian. Judge Wu then questioned the defendant, but the defendant still insisted that he was Brazilian. The court stated that this claim alone was difficult to believe and ordered him to provide evidence such as the language spoken in Brazil and a certificate of nationality. However, the defendant could not speak either Spanish or Portuguese, the two languages spoken in Brazil, and he did not present a certificate of nationality. He only said that the secretary of the Brazilian Consulate, Bai Taili, who was now in court, could testify for him. The court then instructed the defendant's lawyer to ask Bai Taili if he was willing to testify. Bai stated that he was in court to observe on the orders of the Brazilian Consul, and that the Brazilian Consulate had already sent a letter to the court regarding the defendant's nationality issue, and that he was unwilling to testify in a personal capacity. The court stated that since Bai refused to testify and the defendant could not produce any other evidence that could prove his nationality, it ordered both sides' lawyers to debate the nationality issue first. Lawyer Ru then argued extensively, the main points being that the various pieces of evidence submitted by the police were sufficient to prove that the defendant was No. 181, No. 463186, No. 024753, No. 266319, No. 266006, No. 433521; Seventh Prize: last three digits "396," last digit of the first prize "4," last two digits "04."
