Li Xuetang Commits Suicide and a Heartbreaking Suicide Note is Discovered: "Money is an All-Powerful Spiritual Object That Can Overcome Everything;" "The Thinnest Thing in the World is a Beauty's Life"

On the 26th of last month, a young man checked into Room 321 at the Far Eastern Hotel on Xizang Road. He registered as Xue Tang, 18 years old, from Ningbo, a medical practitioner, and later committed suicide by taking poison. The next day, he was discovered by Zhang Zulin, a tea server at the hotel, who reported it to the Laozha Police Station, who ordered detectives to investigate and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, etc., as reported in previous editions of this newspaper. Later, due to the youth's excessive poisoning, treatment was ineffective, and he died from the poison on the previous day. The body was taken to the Fielun Road Morgue for examination. It is now known that detectives have discovered that his name was Li Xuetang and found a suicide note by his side. The tone of the letter was all about economic and romantic troubles. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. After questioning his mother, Li Zhangshi, Guo concluded that the deceased, Li Xuetang, had indeed died from taking an overdose of sleeping pills. The body was handed over to his mother, Li Zhangshi, who signed an undertaking to take it back for burial. Now we have obtained the full text of his suicide note, and we present it here:

"I remember it was three years ago, in the autumn, on the fifteenth afternoon of the lunar September. With a "huhu" sound, that great, merciless ship brought this small, pitiful child from the Yong River to Shanghai. Arriving here, in this wicked city on the sea, seeing the magnificent foreign houses and lightning-fast cars, how enviable! As long as you have money, what does anything else matter? From then on, all vanity entered my mind. When I was resentful, I comforted myself, as long as unexpected wealth came rolling in, what hardship would matter? Time flies quickly over everyone's head. Three years have passed. In these three years, I have written a small history, but I do not wish to tell it all. Moreover, my knowledge is very shallow. Some people say I am beautiful. Alas, hearing this hurts me more than a needle pricking my heart, because I know what use is a man's beauty? Money is the all-powerful spiritual object that can overcome everything. What about love? Ha, it's terrible! It's all lies. A fickle and treacherous environment binds me tightly. I have tasted the bitterness of life for several years now. Alas, so bitter! Mother, my dear mother, please do not grieve over my early death. You must know that vessels have their time to break, and life has its end. You should pretend that you never gave birth to this Xue son. And my white-haired grandmother, how can I bear to leave her forever? But I am really forced to do so, alas. Mother, you must comfort her in the future. When a person is in trouble, relatives disappear, and friends do not recognize you. Alas, it can be seen that autumn clouds are as thin as silk, and human feelings are even thinner. The world is cold and ruthless. The thinnest thing in the world is a beauty's life. Father, you must wake up and extricate yourself, and strive in society. Friends, you must wake up and struggle, and take me as a warning. Dear Li, we are separated forever. Do not grieve for me. Your future, your happiness, is waiting for you ahead. As long as you work hard and study the right books. I do not resent anything, only hate the Creator, Heaven. He has been too unfair in giving me luck. Xue Tang, 23.2.26, midnight."

National Children's Year Postponed to Next Year: National Government Has Already Ordered the Child Welfare Association; Shanghai Will Still Proceed Independently

The China Child Welfare Association previously received a letter from the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee requesting the National Government to issue a nationwide order designating this year as Children's Year in order to awaken public attention and raise the inherent status of children. Now it has received a directive from the National Government, forwarded by the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, changing the designation to 1935 as Children's Year in order to allow for full preparation and enthusiastic celebration. However, according to a standing committee member of the Shanghai Municipal Children's Committee, the committee has already been approved by the Municipal Government to proceed independently as planned, and may also participate next year. The directive is excerpted below.

Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Directive Hui Zi No. 1025:

Regarding the matter of the Association's request to the Municipal Government to designate 1934 as Children's Year, it has been reviewed and endorsed as a case. Now, National Government Directive No. 8553 states, "Previously, the China Child Welfare Association requested, through the Bureau, the National Government's review and approval to designate 1934 as Children's Year, which has been submitted and approved. Now, National Government Civil Service Office Letter No. 475 states, 'Regarding the case of the Municipal Government's previous submission, through the Social Affairs Bureau, of the China Child Welfare Association's request to designate 1934 as Children's Year, it has been submitted to the Executive Yuan, and a reply has been approved, stating that the matter has been referred to the Ministries of Interior and Education. Now, the Ministry of Education's response states, 'The Association's submission is for the purpose of arousing nationwide public attention to children's welfare, and the implementation measures are practical and detailed, and seem feasible. However, the holding of Children's Year requires full preparation for all pre-event planning and implementation steps. The request to designate 1934 as Children's Year is noted, but since many days have already passed this year, it is inconvenient. If the designation is changed to 1935 as Children's Year, and preparations begin this year, all measures for Children's Year will be more convenient to implement, etc.' It is deemed that the Ministry's proposal is appropriate and should be approved accordingly. In addition to ordering the Ministry of Interior to be informed, this reply is for your reference and compliance.' Accordingly, this directive is hereby issued for the Bureau to forward to the Association for compliance."

In light of this, this directive is hereby issued for the Association to comply.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Two Roads Administration Requesting the Preservation of the Small Wooden Bridge at Panjiawan

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce wrote to the Two Roads Administration yesterday, stating:

"We are writing regarding the joint letter from eleven merchants at the Dah Yang Bridge in Zhabei, including Hesheng Xieji Rice Shop, Yang Wanxing, Qingda, and Shen Zhaofeng Noodles Shop, stating that their businesses at the Dah Yang Bridge depend on a small wooden bridge crossing the railway to reach Panjiawan to the south. Over ten thousand people travel back and forth daily, making the Dah Yang Bridge and Panjiawan prosperous in commerce and industry. The importance of this wooden bridge was recognized by previous directors, who preserved it on record. Now, the Roads Administration, without fully considering local conditions, intends to demolish the wooden bridge, blocking traffic and threatening the livelihoods of thousands of merchants and laborers. They have repeatedly requested preservation but have not been granted approval. This matter concerns local livelihoods and merchants' interests. We earnestly request that your esteemed Chamber provide assistance by writing to the Roads Administration to refrain from demolishing the wooden bridge, to maintain commerce and benefit the people."

In light of this, the small wooden bridge is a crucial thoroughfare for traffic north and south of the railway, serving as a link for Panjiawan's commerce. Past Roads Administration directors have preserved it to this day, facilitating industry and commerce. If it is demolished suddenly, it will have a significant impact on commercial exchange in the area. Accordingly, we are writing to request that your esteemed Administration review this matter, consider that the small wooden bridge is vital to the prosperity of Panjiawan, and refrain from demolishing it, to solidify our public friendship.

The Beginning and End of the Establishment of the Sacred Heart Hospital by Lu Bohong and Others: Adding a New-Style Hospital with an Attached Maternity Hospital; Inauguration Scheduled for 3 PM Today.

In the summer of the founding of the Republic, Shanghai philanthropist and current President of the Chinese Catholic Action General Association, Lu Bohong, and others, in view of the fact that the Yangshupu area was densely populated with factories and workers often suffered from illness and lacked funds for medical treatment, rented several houses nearby and invited Franciscan nuns to provide medical care and medicine. Every day, five or six hundred people came seeking treatment. In 1923, because the rented houses were insufficient, Mr. Lu and other Chinese and foreign Catholic philanthropists raised funds to purchase more than 60 mu of land on Ningguo Road and built new-style male and female wards, a total of five buildings, divided into special, first, second, third, and fourth classes. There was also a kindergarten. Each ward could accommodate 120 people. Subsequently, in cooperation with the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee, the hospital purchased from France all the newly invented radium therapy equipment for the specialized treatment of various cancers and difficult diseases, worth more than 200,000 yuan. The radium alone was valued at more than 100,000 yuan and was the first of its kind in East Asia, as other hospitals did not have such equipment. The hospital also had a large and small X-ray machine, which had strong therapeutic power and about three effects: (1) diagnosing the actual condition of various internal diseases; (2) taking photos to prove the location of the disease; (3) treating scrofula, lung disease, etc. Currently, the hospital's medical committee chairman is Shi Deli, the medical director is Song Wusheng, and the resident doctors for internal and external medicine are Pan Weicen and Hou Yunqing. The radium director is Ge Chengzhi, and the X-ray director is Zhang Youmei. Special doctors for internal, external, obstetrics, pediatrics, forensic medicine are Dr. Xie Bide and the Dr. Luo siblings, volunteer doctors for internal, external, obstetrics, pediatrics, and pulmonary medicine are Mude, and for pulmonary medicine, Auyi Bumei, internal and external medicine German doctor Engel, and doctors with European medical doctorates such as internal and external medicine Xie Yingrui, surgery Huang Wen Er, eye, nose, and throat Liu Zunzhu, skin and venereal disease Chen Bangdian, internal and external medicine Cai Hong, etc., are all leaders in the Chinese and foreign medical communities in Shanghai. The hospital also saw an increasing number of patients, and the original wards could not meet the demand. Therefore, it borrowed funds to add a new-style three-story steel-concrete building with a special-class ward that could accommodate 120 people, and an attached maternity hospital. The internal equipment was all modern and scientific. The architecture was planned by Mr. Lu's son, Lu Yigeng, and the drawings were designed by architect Li Wen in conjunction with Qian Shaoping of the Dongya Construction Company, and constructed by Wang Caihong of the Qia Xing Construction Company. The construction is now complete and the opening ceremony is scheduled for 3 PM today. Bishop Hui of the Shanghai District will be invited to preside over the ceremony, and Mr. Lu will invite guests from all walks of life to visit. It is reported that Mayor Wu and various bureau chiefs, as well as the General Directors of the British and French Municipal Councils, will also attend the ceremony. At that time, Ningguo Road will be crowded with traffic and there will be a grand occasion.

Another Fire Near the Sun Temple on Jiaotong Road: More Than 40 Straw Houses Destroyed

Due to the dry weather in recent days, fires have been frequent. On the morning of the previous day, a fire broke out in the straw houses of poor people behind Xiangyuan Lane on Zhangqiao Road in Zhabei, resulting in the destruction of more than 50 straw houses. Unexpectedly, at around 4 AM yesterday, another fire broke out on Jiaotong Road behind the Sun Temple in Zhabei. It turned out that Li Jucai, a man from Jiangbei, worked as a laborer and lived in a straw house for the poor behind the Jiaotong Road Sun Temple. At around 4 AM yesterday, Li got up to cook porridge for breakfast because he was going to work at the factory at around 5 AM. Unexpectedly, he accidentally left the embers in the stove on the rice straw next to the stove, causing a fire. The flames quickly rose and the fire lit up the sky, soon piercing the roof and spreading to the neighbors. A group of residents were awakened from their dreams and rushed out, carrying boxes and baskets, fighting to escape, with a loud noise, the order was chaotic. The nearby police substation in the fourth district heard the news and quickly notified the fire brigade, at the same time rushing dispatching police officers to maintain order. Fire brigades responded to the news, rushing fire trucks to the scene to put out the fire, but by this time more than 40 straw houses had already been burned down, and the fire had spread to two flat houses at No. 26 nearby. Firefighters were forced to try and prevent it from spreading further, while also putting out the fire. By around 5 AM, the fire was finally extinguished, although the losses were not large, the situation was very tragic, and many victims were in a sorry state, sitting on the ground, facing the scene of the disaster, tears streaming down their faces, Li Jucai, who caused the fire, was arrested by the police and taken to the district office for interrogation.

Anhui People Secretly Set Up a Gambling Den and Were Arrested: No. 2 Wu Jia Lane in the Old North Gate, recently some Anhui people secretly set up a gambling den inside, with Pai Gow mahjong and all kinds of gambling, also leaving a group to entice shop employees to gamble, they profited from the rake-off, yesterday morning at around 2 AM, after the first division of the second district got an intelligence report, Director Shen immediately dispatched Police Chief Ma Yumin, Gao Kui, and police officers Niu Zhenqing, Mu Zhenjiang, etc. in disguise as gamblers, just as all the gamblers were excitedly pushing Pai Gow, Police Chief Ma gave a signal, arresting them, due to there being many gamblers, several people escaped, counting 21 people on the spot that were arrested Wu Kenan etc, along with gambling equipment, notes, cash, corner tickets, etc., all taken to the police station for investigation, after Director Shen interrogated, he found that the case involved gathering for gambling and disrupting public safety, and planned to send them to the bureau to be dealt with according to law.

Unable to Bear the Pain of Illness, Committed Suicide by Inhaling Smoke: Cao Yongdi, a 50-year-old local resident who owned a stove shop at No. 33 Tao Sha Chang Street in the city, had recently been suffering from hemorrhoids, constipation, and severe pain. He had the idea of dying, and at around 6 PM yesterday, he secretly inhaled a large amount of smoke behind people's backs and committed suicide. He was later discovered and rushed to Renji Hospital by car, but he died soon after, unable to be cured.

Argument Between Husband and Wife, Wife Took Poison: Gong Huangshi, a 32-year-old woman from Suzhou, lived with her husband, Gong Jianliang, at No. 61 Boer Road, Avenue Joffre. Usually, the relationship between the couple was very good. Yesterday at around 10 AM, for some reason, she had an argument with her husband. Afterwards, she was very angry and suddenly had the idea of dying, so she secretly took 40 sleeping pills and committed suicide. She was later discovered by her family and immediately taken to the hospital for treatment by car. It is said that she had been poisoned deeply and her life may be in danger.

Performed a Robbery Wedding due to Lack of Money to Pay the Bride Price: Shen Fushi, an old woman living in a thatched shed on Hengfeng Road in Zhabei, has two sons and a daughter. The sons, Shen Hongzhen and Shen Xiaoxizi, both work for a living. The daughter, Shen Qiaozhen, is 21 years old and of good appearance. Since childhood, she was promised in marriage through matchmakers Xu Yujiang, Chen Chenmao, Ni Zhentong, Fu Daishi, etc., to Wang Zhilan, the son of Wang Fanglai, a fellow villager from Xie Xing Lane, Nanjing Street, Hai Chao Temple in the South City. Zhilan is 26 years old this year and used to pull a rickshaw. Now that the man has grown and the daughter is old, it is time for them to get married. The original matchmakers were asked to arrange the wedding, and it was agreed that the bride would be married after the betrothal gifts were exchanged the day before yesterday. The bride's family asked for a bride price of 140 yuan, but the groom's family asked to reduce it, so the matter was not resolved. The groom's family then pretended to agree and secretly planned to hire a car and gather relatives and friends to fake the betrothal gifts. When they arrived at the bride's house, the betrothal gifts were empty, but a group of strong men rushed in and forcibly robbed Shen Qiaozhen, putting her in the car and carrying out the robbery wedding. Shen Fushi's two sons were shocked and immediately stepped forward to resist, and a fight broke out. At the same time, the police whistle blew and the police rushed to the scene. The people who helped with the wedding robbery got in the car and fled. The Wang father and son were grabbed by Shen Fushi and others and taken into custody at the second precinct of the fourth district. Under interrogation, the Wang father and son claimed that they disliked poverty and relied on marriage, and that poor people had no choice but to resort to this tactic, etc. Because the matter could not be resolved, it was submitted to the third sub-section and transferred to the prosecutor's office of the district court for investigation according to law.

Li Guocheng, Who Was Sentenced to Death, Filed an Appeal:

On the evening of August 15, 1931, at around 6 PM, in Room 2 of the Fa Shang Hotel at No. 113 Xinxinqiao Street, French Concession, a Jiangbei bandit murdered his accomplices, shooting and killing Jiang Zonghan, Xia Yongsheng, and a man named Xue, and wounding Zhong Ziqing. Qian Yumin, a detective from the French police station, solved the case the next day, arresting the criminal Yan Jinbiao from Funing and handing him over to the Second Special Court, which sentenced him to death. The criminal refused to accept the sentence and appealed repeatedly. After three trials, the original sentence was upheld, and he was executed on April 6 of last year. After Yan was arrested, he confessed that Li Guocheng, also known as Chen Youliang, a fellow villager who was at large, was the mastermind and that they went to commit the murder together. Later, Yan's family arrested Li in the Rihui Port area of Shanghai South and sent him to the Public Security Bureau. The Special Second Court brought him back and handed him over to the French police station for investigation and prosecution. After investigating the evidence, he was sentenced to death in December of last year for jointly conspiring to commit murder. Li refused to accept the original sentence and hired lawyers Zhang Shijie and Shen Yushan to file an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, as reported in previous newspapers. It is learned that the main points of Li's appeal are: "When this case occurred, I was in my hometown of Gou Dun Town with the police squad leader Ma Buwen handling bandit suppression work, and I was not in Shanghai. The original trial only believed Yan Jinbiao's confession and imposed a heavy sentence. Moreover, Jiang Zonghan pointed out Yan during his pre-death statement in the hospital, but did not point out that I was also at the scene of the murder. Moreover, there are several contradictions in Yan's confession that do not match the facts. I am truly unwilling to accept this and request that the injustice be redressed." February Coinage of 3.9 Million

The Central Mint Inspection Committee issued Announcement No. 9 the other day, stating that the new coins of 3.9 million yuan submitted by the Central Mint for inspection in February of this year have been inspected by the chemist Mr. Ge Laide, appointed by the Committee, in accordance with the regulations. The fineness and weight were in compliance with the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations, and certificates were issued from No. 5963 to No. 6742. In addition, the Class B factory bars (880 fineness) manufactured by the Central Mint in February, from No. 3058 to No. 6515, totaling 3,458 bars, were also monitored and stamped by the chemist Mr. Ge Laide, appointed by the Committee, during their "calibration marking," and the fineness and weight of each bar were listed and registered. In addition to being allowed to leave the factory separately, this announcement is hereby made.

North-

British, American, and French Air Forces 61

England Increases Four Squadrons, One Stationed in Singapore

America Adds 1,000 Fighter Planes

France Also Strives to Modernize its Air Force

(London) The 1934 British Air Force budget stipulates an increase of four aircraft squadrons. The annual expenditure is £17,561,000, an increase of £135,000 compared to the previous year. Among the four newly added squadrons, one is a flying boat squadron, which will be stationed overseas. The remaining three squadrons will: one, join the naval fleet air force; and two, be used for domestic defense. After this increase, the Royal Air Force will have a total of eighty-one permanent squadrons and thirteen non-permanent squadrons. The Air Minister, Marquess of Londonderry, mentioned the budget today, stating that the US government intends to avoid an air force arms race at all costs. While the results of the disarmament conference are still undecided, the number of new military positions in Britain has been reduced to the minimum. However, for the sake of national and imperial security, the British government cannot continue to accept a position where its air force is inferior to other countries. (2nd, Reuters)

(London) The budget for British naval aviation expenditures, starting from April 1st of this year, has been released today, totaling £20,165,600, an increase of £527,000 compared to the previous term. An explanation from the Aviation Minister is attached, stating that the British Air Force is purely for self-defense. Now that several countries are expanding their air forces daily, Britain appears to be falling behind. This term's budget shows a slight increase. Cabinet members have repeatedly demonstrated Britain's sincerity in achieving air force disarmament, but for the sake of imperial security, the British Air Force cannot be inferior to other countries. Therefore, it is planned to add four new aircraft squadrons in the next fiscal year, each squadron limited to nine to twelve aircraft, making a total of eighty-one squadrons in the Royal Air Force. One squadron is entirely composed of flying boats and will be stationed overseas. Rumor has it that the squadron will be sent to Singapore, in accordance with the recent resolutions of the Singapore Naval Conference. (2nd, National Telegram)

(Washington) The proposal to add 3,000 army aircraft was refuted this morning by Secretary of War Dern in a statement. However, the Secretary of War supports the resolution proposed by Congressman McSwain, which is now set to add 1,000 fighter planes and recruit 400 officers and 6,200 soldiers for the Army Air Corps, as part of the five-year plan proposed by the Army General Staff. The resolution is currently under consideration by the House Military Affairs Committee and will soon be presented in a report. (1st, National Telegram)

(Paris) Reuters learned today that France has no intention of increasing its air force. The reports in the newspapers are unreliable. France has already reduced eight air force squadrons in the past few months. The current reorganization is merely to modernize the air force. (1st, Reuters)

Japanese Air Combat Exercise 62

Continuous for Five Days Starting from the 13th

Fifty-Nine Aircraft Participating

(Tokyo) According to the Japanese Army Ministry, the Air Force has decided to conduct an exercise of air force formation combat in the area between Kakamigahara and Ichinomiya for five days starting from the 13th. The participating units are the Tachikawa Air Corps, the Otabaru Air Corps, the Hamamatsu Air Corps, and the Hamamatsu Flying School, etc. The aircraft used are as follows: "Twenty-seven Type 91 fighters, eighteen Type 92 fighters, ten light bombers, and four heavy bombers," totaling fifty-nine aircraft participating, with the main purpose of training in air combat and aerial bombing. (2nd, China United Press)

Austria Forms Elite Troops 63

Army Increased to 120,000

Deputy Prime Minister Fey's Ambition

While Vienna attracts Europe's attention, Austria has quietly increased its army from 30,000 to 120,000 men, either directly under the regular army or with organizations easily converted into regular army status, based on the Treaty of Saint-Germain. Austrian Deputy Prime Minister Fey presided over the expansion ceremony of the auxiliary army yesterday, which increased the number of officers by fifteen and soldiers by three thousand. Deputy Prime Minister Fey's newspaper estimates that the strength of the Austrian Home Guard (Fascist Party) and the Allied Forces is a total of 60,000 men, plus the 30,000 men of the regular army allowed by the treaty, and about 10,000 policemen and gendarmes, who are generally recruited from soldiers of the regular army and are easily converted into regular army troops. From this, it can be seen that Austria can now place elite troops on the battlefield. (1st, Reuters)

Vienna The verbal ultimatum from the German Habicht to Austria has now exceeded its deadline by one day. The entire territory of Austria is still peaceful, but the focus of attention is currently on tomorrow's meeting of the leaders of the "Patriotic Front," which will be held at the same time as the cabinet meeting. (1st, Reuters)

Vienna The investigation into the recent Socialist Party uprising has been completed. The Chief Prosecutor has recently filed charges against the former Mayor of Vienna, Seitz, the former Prime Minister Renner, Congressman Danneberg, Ellerbogen, and sixteen other leaders of the Socialist Party. Although the charges are for treason, they will still be tried in ordinary courts. Among the sixteen Socialist Party leaders, Bauer and Eder have fled abroad. (1st, Havas)

Vienna Most of the staff of the Socialist Party Defense Force are former officers of the Austro-Hungarian Empire, such as General Knauss, General Schneller, Major Evertlow, and Captain Liu, and so on. These officers were detained in court last night and will be charged with treason. (2nd, Havas)

Conference of Italy, Austria, and Hungary 64

Held in Rome on March 12th

Rome The tripartite meeting to be held in Rome soon, involving Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös, and Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss, is scheduled for around March 12th. Italian newspapers still say that the Italian public has not received official news about this matter, but only learned about the meeting from foreign dispatches from Vienna and London. (2nd, National Telegram)

Germany and Bulgaria Rebuild Old Ties 65

Bulgarian King in Secret Talks with Hitler

(Berlin) Although the King of Bulgaria's visit to Berlin is officially stated to have no political purpose, the fact is that the King went to Berlin and personally met with various important figures in the German authorities, gaining an understanding of all the policies and figures of Germany after the reforms. This point is extremely important. The King visited German Foreign Minister Neurath this afternoon and had a long conversation for two hours. Then he attended the banquet of President Hindenburg. During the meeting, the King had a long conversation with the German President, detailing Bulgaria's current political strategy. During the banquet, President Hindenburg raised his glass in tribute, saying, "In my declining years, I am very pleased to meet the young and handsome King of Bulgaria. In these difficult times, Your Majesty is still able to manage affairs with ease and has achieved remarkable political results. I offer you German wine as a tribute and wish you good health." After the banquet, the King and Chancellor Hitler left for a meeting lasting about an hour. The King inquired in detail about the current political views of the National Socialist Party and the achievements of the various measures it has already implemented. During the discussions, there was no argument. Afterwards, Chancellor Hitler said that he would personally pay his respects to the King at his residence to express his greetings. The King was modest and said that the Chancellor was very busy with government affairs and would pay his respects first. Thus, a date was set and they parted. These several meetings will certainly make the friendship between the two countries even more solid. (1st, National Telegram)

Saar Parties Merge 66

Organize the German Front Movement

The Entire Territory is Covered with the German Swastika Flag

Saarbrücken, March 1st, marks a new era in the history of the Saar region, because today the various political parties here have automatically merged, issued a joint declaration, and organized a united movement called the "German Front Movement," whose purpose is for the Saar region to belong to Germany, as the slogan says, "Our Germany," to fight for unity. The declaration has been unanimously disclosed by all newspapers in the Saar region today, stating that whether it is the Social Democratic Party, the Communist Party, the Center Party, the National Socialist Party, or the trade union organizations, they were once hostile organizations, but today they all stand under the same banner of "Our Germany." Today is the time to start working hard, and the final victory will surely belong to our German Front. The houses throughout the Saar region are covered with the German swastika emblem today. (1st, National Telegram)

Anglo-American Peaceful Cooperation 67

American Ambassador Bingham Returns to London

Talks About the American Recovery Situation

(London) The US Ambassador to London, Bingham, has recently returned home. It is said that since last year, the changes in the American situation are almost unbelievable. Credit has been greatly restored, which can be directly evidenced by the large companies' profits and the sharp decline in unemployment. The abolition of prohibition has greatly contributed to the general recovery. President Roosevelt has received unprecedented support from the people, and the cooperation of Congress has never been seen before in American history. All efforts are focused on maintaining world peace. Bingham concluded that the British and American governments are now managing everything with sincerity and harmonious cooperation. (2nd, Reuters)

Anglo-Japanese Cotton Industry Negotiations on the Verge of Collapse 68

Japan Considers Withdrawing its Representatives

Further Diplomatic Negotiations to be Conducted

Osaka The Anglo-Japanese Cotton Industry Consultation will hold its fourth meeting on the 7th. However, according to the current situation, the meeting is on the verge of collapse. The collapse of the consultation will not only have a major impact on the spinning industry of both countries, but also have repercussions on the entire trade relationship between England and Japan. Therefore, the timing of the Japanese delegation's withdrawal and the aftermath are being carefully considered by the Japanese authorities. According to the opinions of key figures in the Japan Spinners' Association, the methods to break the deadlock are as follows: (1) The people's consultation should take the fourth consultation as the final meeting, temporarily suspend negotiations, and allow diplomatic negotiations between the British and Japanese governments to change the situation. (2) The Japanese delegation should temporarily withdraw from London and seek compromise methods after a certain period of time. (2nd, Japan United Press)

Manchester The Anglo-Japanese textile industry talks are currently at a standstill due to the scope of the meeting. The cotton industry here has a very firm attitude on this matter. The Manchester Chamber of Commerce's monthly publication for March states that all countries feel the intensity of Japanese competition and are willing to recognize Japan as a competitor under appropriate conditions, but Japan cannot have reasons to harm others. The current negotiation is a touchstone for Japanese economic policy. If an agreement is not reached, repercussions will inevitably arise. Both parties should be aware of the possibility of these repercussions and quickly seek a solution. (2nd, Reuters)

Anti-Japanese Atmosphere in the Dutch East Indies is Intense 69

From Economic Reasons to Politicization

The Japanese Government Plans Countermeasures

Osaka According to a telegram received today by a Japanese merchant from Surabaya, the Dutch government has implemented restrictions on the import of foreign cotton cloth since yesterday, using 1928 as the standard. It stipulates the import of cotton yarn and cloth from various countries, with the Dutch occupying 60%, other European and American goods occupying 30%, and others 10%. The intention is entirely to prevent the dumping of Japanese cotton cloth. Although it is said to be a temporary measure for ten months, Japanese merchants will suffer considerable losses. Furthermore, there are recent plans to restrict other Japanese goods. The Dutch government's actions are not only for economic reasons, but also have political implications. Recently, Dutch officials and merchants have been very resentful of the dumping of Japanese goods, which has led to an anti-Japanese atmosphere. It is heard that Japanese merchants intend to petition the government, asking it to lodge a serious protest with the Dutch government and demand that the Dutch government ease the anti-Japanese atmosphere. (2nd, China United Press)

(Tokyo) Due to the Dutch East Indies' restrictions on the import of Japanese cotton cloth, the Director of the Commerce Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Kurasu, the Director of the Information Section of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, Oshima, and more than ten important officials from the two ministries held a meeting at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 2:00 pm today. The ministries presented reference materials, and after discussing for two hours, no conclusion was reached. It was decided to hold another meeting at 2:00 pm on the 9th to review and determine countermeasures. (2nd, China United Press)

Portuguese Merchants Request the Government to Abolish the Portuguese-Japanese Commercial Treaty 70

To Prevent the Dumping of Japanese Cotton Cloth

(Tokyo) The Tokyo Newspaper reports that Portuguese cotton merchants have suffered considerable losses due to the dumping of Japanese goods in Portugal, which has harmed the country's industry. Due to the Portuguese-Japanese Commercial Treaty, it is inconvenient to raise tariffs for defense. The Madrid Chamber of Commerce submitted a proposal to the government on March 1st, requesting the government to abolish the Portuguese-Japanese Commercial Treaty to protect the country's industry. (2nd, China United Press)

British House of Commons Debates the Anglo-Russian Commercial Treaty 71

Unemployed Demonstrators Suddenly Demonstrate in the Parliament

Shouting "Down with the Government" Slogans

Released Only After Being Confined in a Room

London Secretary of Commerce Runciman explained the significance of the recently completed Anglo-Russian Commercial Treaty in the House of Commons today. It is said that the significance of this agreement is to correct the imbalance of trade between the two countries. The British side believes that if Russia cannot buy more British goods in England, then Britain cannot buy more Russian goods either. Soviet Russia has accepted this view and at the same time acknowledged that the British side has the right to prohibit the import of Russian goods when Russian goods prices disrupt the Ottawa Conference Agreement. Recently, a representative of the Lena Goldfields went to Moscow, and there is a possibility of resolving the company's claim for compensation for losses against the Russian government. Up to now, all payments for British goods shipped to Russia have been paid promptly. Even when six British technicians were arrested by the Russian authorities, causing a suspension of trade between the two countries, the payments were still made as usual. Runciman concluded that this type of payment will continue. (1st, Reuters)

(London) Some of the unemployed who arrived in London at the end of last week entered the gallery of the House of Commons during dinner tonight. When the House of Commons was debating the Anglo-Russian Commercial Treaty, these uninvited guests suddenly took demonstration actions, which hindered the proceedings of the meeting. The unemployed shouted slogans such as "Down with the Government." Six people were dragged out by the police. An hour later, shouts were heard again in the gallery, and the police dragged seven more troublemakers out of the venue. According to custom, the demonstrators were all confined to a separate room, and after the adjournment of the meeting, they were escorted to the street and released one by one. (1st, Reuters)

(London) Tonight, when the House of Commons was discussing the newly signed Anglo-Russian Commercial Treaty, some unknown people suddenly stood up from the gallery and hurled abuse, shouting "Down with the government that creates starvation." Most people echoed in unison. A woman repeatedly shouted "Long live the Soviet Union." The officials on duty in the parliament and the police intervened, and fought with those who disturbed the order. As a result, they were finally expelled. This demonstration action seemed to be organized in advance. Its purpose was to protest against the House of Commons' refusal to meet with the representatives of the hunger marchers. (1st, Havas)

Italian-Dutch and German-Danish Commercial Treaties Signed on the Same Day 72

Rome The new commercial treaty between Italy and the Netherlands was signed here today. Germany and Denmark also concluded a new commercial treaty in Copenhagen today. (2nd, Reuters)

US Treasury Secretary's Statement 73

The Experimental Monetary Policy Will Not be Stopped for the Time Being

Hoping that Related Countries Will Approve the Silver Agreement

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau told the House Appropriations Subcommittee today that he intends to continue the current experimental monetary policy, at least until the end of this fiscal year. He said that although he could not say for sure what special impact the silver purchasing program would have on world silver prices or the purchasing power of other countries, he was convinced that if all related countries approved the London Silver Agreement, it would have a beneficial impact. The House Appropriations Subcommittee is currently studying a proposal to establish a central agency with the exclusive right to issue currency. (1st, Reuters)

Germany and Poland Reach a Customs Truce Agreement 74

Mutual Abandonment of Import Restrictions

Shipping and Transportation Also Involved

Berlin The customs war between Germany and Poland has stopped, as the two countries have reached an agreement to abandon mutual import restrictions. The new agreement will be signed within the next week, and German-Polish relations will be further improved as a result. The new agreement allows the export of certain Polish grain products to Germany that were previously prohibited, and the export of various German products to Poland will also increase, without specifying quotas. The new agreement also involves shipping and transportation matters. (1st, National Telegram)

Wife of the Main Culprit in the French Fraud Case Imprisoned 75

Possession of her Husband's Checkbook Stubs

Paris The wife of Stavisky, the main culprit in the Bayonne Municipal Credit Bank fraud case, was arrested this morning. The main reason for her arrest was that the prosecutor of the Seine Court proved that Stavisky's wife had stubs of checks issued by her husband and other documents that the judicial authorities were searching for. The prosecutor also received a reliable report that Stavisky's wife intended to flee France, so the prosecutor issued a summons today for Stavisky's wife to appear in court. She was accused by the prosecutor of suspicion of conspiracy with Stavisky in the fraud case and harboring stolen goods. During the interrogation, the defendant denied possessing suspicious documents, but the prosecutor was not satisfied and sent the defendant to prison. Also, during the cabinet meeting this morning, Interior Minister Sarraut declared that the checkbook stubs signed by Stavisky, which were seized by the authorities yesterday, had been stamped and sealed. After being checked one by one, they were immediately transferred to the congressional investigative committee for verification. This afternoon, the stubs were photographed and preserved. (2nd, Havas)

The Spanish Cabinet Crisis is Not Easy to Resolve 76

Left and Right Factions Compete for Power

Madrid The Spanish cabinet crisis has not yet been resolved, but it is widely believed that Lerroux will still form a right-wing cabinet. However, the newspapers of the left-wing claim that if the right-wing forms a cabinet, it will lead to civil war. (2nd, National Telegram)

Madrid The Lerroux cabinet has lost the support of the right-wing Catholic party. President Zamora recently met with the current Speaker of the House, Alba, and the former Speaker, Besteiro, to seek their opinions. The two suggested that Lerroux be asked to form a cabinet again, and that the new government should be based on a broad majority party in Congress. The Radical Party believes that the President will still entrust Lerroux to form a cabinet, but it is heard that former Prime Minister Azaña and most of the left-wing have decided to adopt a clear revolutionary attitude and carry out a vigorous movement in the hope of dissolving Congress and preventing the right-wing from taking power. (1st, Havas)

Anglo-American Exchange Rate In the London foreign exchange market, due to little trading, the pound sterling gradually improved. The opening rate for Anglo-French exchange was 77.31 francs, a decrease of 3 points compared to yesterday's closing rate. Before noon, it fluctuated between 77.40 francs and 77.28 francs. New York Market Conditions 80

Securities Yesterday's closing was slightly higher, and it was still able to expand today, so the opening was stable, especially for railway, copper, iron, and petroleum securities. However, there was not much trading. Many expect the market conditions to continue to fluctuate.

Cotton Market sentiment was mixed at the opening today, but it rose due to professional purchases to cover short positions and purchases by Japanese merchants. The sentiment gradually became optimistic. However, people in the industry are still waiting for developments in Washington.

Silver The opening was sluggish, with a loosening trend. Sentiment was uncertain. There was some selling pressure later, as it was heard that China's approval of the London Silver Agreement would depend on whether the stability of the silver market was being observed.

Rubber Market conditions were sluggish, with a tendency to loosen along with London news.

Japanese Consulate in Nanjing Has Not Established a Police Station 84

(Nanjing) Recently, it was reported that the Japanese Consulate in Nanjing would establish a police station. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs inquired with the Japanese side. According to the reply, there is no police station, but one or two additional staff members will be added to be responsible for protection and to crack down on Japanese residents. Because when unscrupulous Japanese residents commit crimes and are arrested, and the Chinese police hand them over to the Japanese Consulate, ordinary staff members find it difficult to cope, so additional staff members are added to take on the responsibility. (Nanjing) A key member of the Yangtze River Conservancy Commission said that the Chairman of the Commission, Zhao Zhiyou, plans to expand the number of committee members by adding the heads of construction departments from the six provinces along the river, so that talent and financial resources can be concentrated.
